(**********************************************************************************

 The double category of spans

 In this file, we define the double category of spans. If `C` is a category with
 pullbacks, then we have the following double category:
 - Objects: objects in `C`
 - Vertical morphisms: morphisms in `C`
 - Horizontal morphisms: spans in `C`
 - Squares: morphisms of spans
 Spans are composed by taking a pullback.

 Contents
 1. Horizontal identities
 2. Horizontal composition
 3. The unitors and associators
 4. The triangle and pentagon equations
 5. The double category of spans

 **********************************************************************************)

Notation "_ ≠ _" was already used in scope nat_scope.

  (** * 1. Horizontal identities *)

hor_id_data (twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C)

C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
∏ (x y : C) (f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧), ?I x -->[ f ][ f] ?I y

    
C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
∏ x : C, twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x x
 exact (id_span C).
    
C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
∏ (x y : C) (f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧),
id_span C x -->[ f ][ f] id_span C y
 exact (λ x y f, id_span_mor C f).
  Defined.

∏ x : C,
double_id_mor spans_double_cat_hor_id_data (id₁ x) =

C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
∏ (x y z : C) (f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧) (g : C ⟦ y, z ⟧),
double_id_mor spans_double_cat_hor_id_data (f · g) =
double_id_mor spans_double_cat_hor_id_data f ;;2 double_id_mor
                                                 spans_double_cat_hor_id_data
                                                 g

a: C

      apply idpath.
  Qed.

PC: Pullbacks C

twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x y
→ twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y z
  → twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x z
C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
∏ (x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ z₁ z₂ : C) (v₁ : C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧)
(v₂ : C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧) (v₃ : C ⟦ z₁, z₂ ⟧)
(h₁ : twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₁ y₁)
(h₂ : twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y₁ z₁)
(k₁ : twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₂ y₂)
(k₂ : twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y₂ z₂),
h₁ -->[ v₁ ][ v₂] k₁
→ h₂ -->[ v₂ ][ v₃] k₂
  → ?Cm x₁ y₁ z₁ h₁ h₂ -->[ v₁
    ][ v₃] ?Cm x₂ y₂ z₂ k₁ k₂

    
C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
∏ x y z : C,
twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x y
→ twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y z
  → twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x z
 exact (λ a₁ a₂ a₃ s t, comp_span C PC s t).
    
C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
∏ (x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ z₁ z₂ : C) (v₁ : C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧)
(v₂ : C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧) (v₃ : C ⟦ z₁, z₂ ⟧)
(h₁ : twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₁ y₁)
(h₂ : twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y₁ z₁)
(k₁ : twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₂ y₂)
(k₂ : twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y₂ z₂),
h₁ -->[ v₁ ][ v₂] k₁
→ h₂ -->[ v₂ ][ v₃] k₂
  → (λ (a₁ a₂ a₃ : C)
     (s : twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C a₁ a₂)
     (t : twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C a₂ a₃),
     comp_span C PC s t) x₁ y₁ z₁ h₁ h₂ -->[ v₁
    ][ v₃] (λ (a₁ a₂ a₃ : C)
            (s : twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C a₁ a₂)
            (t : twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C a₂ a₃),
            comp_span C PC s t) x₂ y₂ z₂ k₁ k₂
 exact (λ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ s₁ s₂, comp_span_mor C PC s₁ s₂).
  Defined.

C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
∏ (x y z : C) (h₁ : twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x y)
(h₂ : twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y z),
double_hor_comp_mor spans_double_cat_hor_comp_data
  (id_two_disp h₁) (id_two_disp h₂) =
id_two_disp
  (double_hor_comp spans_double_cat_hor_comp_data h₁
     h₂)
C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
∏ (x₁ x₂ x₃ y₁ y₂ y₃ z₁ z₂ z₃ : C) (v₁ : C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧)
(v₁' : C ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧) (v₂ : C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧)
(v₂' : C ⟦ y₂, y₃ ⟧) (v₃ : C ⟦ z₁, z₂ ⟧)
(v₃' : C ⟦ z₂, z₃ ⟧)
(h₁ : twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₁ y₁)
(h₂ : twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y₁ z₁)
(k₁ : twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₂ y₂)
(k₂ : twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y₂ z₂)
(l₁ : twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₃ y₃)
(l₂ : twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y₃ z₃)
(s₁ : h₁ -->[ v₁ ][ v₂] k₁)
(s₁' : k₁ -->[ v₁' ][ v₂'] l₁)
(s₂ : h₂ -->[ v₂ ][ v₃] k₂)
(s₂' : k₂ -->[ v₂' ][ v₃'] l₂),
double_hor_comp_mor spans_double_cat_hor_comp_data
  (s₁ ;;2 s₁') (s₂ ;;2 s₂') =
double_hor_comp_mor spans_double_cat_hor_comp_data s₁
  s₂ ;;2 double_hor_comp_mor
           spans_double_cat_hor_comp_data s₁' s₂'

  (double_hor_comp spans_double_cat_hor_comp_data h₁

        h₁ h₂))

C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
∏ (x₁ x₂ x₃ y₁ y₂ y₃ z₁ z₂ z₃ : C) (v₁ : C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧)
(v₁' : C ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧) (v₂ : C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧)
(v₂' : C ⟦ y₂, y₃ ⟧) (v₃ : C ⟦ z₁, z₂ ⟧)
(v₃' : C ⟦ z₂, z₃ ⟧)
(h₁ : twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₁ y₁)
(h₂ : twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y₁ z₁)
(k₁ : twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₂ y₂)
(k₂ : twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y₂ z₂)
(l₁ : twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₃ y₃)
(l₂ : twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y₃ z₃)
(s₁ : h₁ -->[ v₁ ][ v₂] k₁)
(s₁' : k₁ -->[ v₁' ][ v₂'] l₁)
(s₂ : h₂ -->[ v₂ ][ v₃] k₂)
(s₂' : k₂ -->[ v₂' ][ v₃'] l₂),
double_hor_comp_mor spans_double_cat_hor_comp_data
  (s₁ ;;2 s₁') (s₂ ;;2 s₂') =
double_hor_comp_mor spans_double_cat_hor_comp_data s₁
  s₂ ;;2 double_hor_comp_mor
           spans_double_cat_hor_comp_data s₁' s₂'
 
C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
x₁, x₂, x₃, y₁, y₂, y₃, z₁, z₂, z₃: C
v₁: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
v₁': C ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
v₂: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
v₂': C ⟦ y₂, y₃ ⟧
v₃: C ⟦ z₁, z₂ ⟧

s₂: h₂ -->[ v₂ ][ v₃] k₂
s₂': k₂ -->[ v₂' ][ v₃'] l₂
double_hor_comp_mor spans_double_cat_hor_comp_data
  (s₁ ;;2 s₁') (s₂ ;;2 s₂') =
double_hor_comp_mor spans_double_cat_hor_comp_data s₁
  s₂ ;;2 double_hor_comp_mor
           spans_double_cat_hor_comp_data s₁' s₂'

x₁, x₂, x₃, y₁, y₂, y₃, z₁, z₂, z₃: C
v₁: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
v₁': C ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
v₂: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
v₂': C ⟦ y₂, y₃ ⟧
v₃: C ⟦ z₁, z₂ ⟧
v₃': C ⟦ z₂, z₃ ⟧
h₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₁ y₁
h₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y₁ z₁
k₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₂ y₂
k₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y₂ z₂
l₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₃ y₃
l₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y₃ z₃
s₁: h₁ -->[ v₁ ][ v₂] k₁
s₁': k₁ -->[ v₁' ][ v₂'] l₁
s₂: h₂ -->[ v₂ ][ v₃] k₂
s₂': k₂ -->[ v₂' ][ v₃'] l₂
mor_of_comp_span_mor C PC
  (pr1 s₁ · pr1 s₁',,
   Core.comp_disp (pr12 s₁) (pr12 s₁'),,
   Core.comp_disp (pr22 s₁) (pr22 s₁'))
  (pr1 s₂ · pr1 s₂',,
   Core.comp_disp (pr12 s₂) (pr12 s₂'),,
   Core.comp_disp (pr22 s₂) (pr22 s₂'))
· PullbackPr2
    (PC y₃ (ob_of_span C l₁) (ob_of_span C l₂)
       (mor_right_of_span C l₁)
       (mor_left_of_span C l₂)) =
mor_of_comp_span_mor C PC s₁ s₂
· (mor_of_comp_span_mor C PC s₁' s₂'
   · PullbackPr2
       (PC y₃ (ob_of_span C l₁) (ob_of_span C l₂)
          (mor_right_of_span C l₁)
          (mor_left_of_span C l₂)))

        
C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
x₁, x₂, x₃, y₁, y₂, y₃, z₁, z₂, z₃: C
v₁: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
v₁': C ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
v₂: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
v₂': C ⟦ y₂, y₃ ⟧
v₃: C ⟦ z₁, z₂ ⟧
v₃': C ⟦ z₂, z₃ ⟧
h₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₁ y₁
h₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y₁ z₁
k₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₂ y₂
k₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y₂ z₂
l₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₃ y₃
l₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y₃ z₃
s₁: h₁ -->[ v₁ ][ v₂] k₁
s₁': k₁ -->[ v₁' ][ v₂'] l₁
s₂: h₂ -->[ v₂ ][ v₃] k₂
s₂': k₂ -->[ v₂' ][ v₃'] l₂
PullbackArrow (comp_span_Pullback C PC l₁ l₂)
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁ h₂)
  (PullbackPr1 (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁ h₂)
   · span_sqr_ob_mor C
       (pr1 s₁ · pr1 s₁',,
        Core.comp_disp (pr12 s₁) (pr12 s₁'),,
        Core.comp_disp (pr22 s₁) (pr22 s₁')))
  (PullbackPr2 (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁ h₂)
   · span_sqr_ob_mor C
       (pr1 s₂ · pr1 s₂',,
        Core.comp_disp (pr12 s₂) (pr12 s₂'),,
        Core.comp_disp (pr22 s₂) (pr22 s₂')))
  (mor_of_comp_span_mor_subproof C PC
     (pr1 s₁ · pr1 s₁',,
      Core.comp_disp (pr12 s₁) (pr12 s₁'),,
      Core.comp_disp (pr22 s₁) (pr22 s₁'))
     (pr1 s₂ · pr1 s₂',,
      Core.comp_disp (pr12 s₂) (pr12 s₂'),,
      Core.comp_disp (pr22 s₂) (pr22 s₂')))
· PullbackPr2
    (PC y₃ (ob_of_span C l₁) (ob_of_span C l₂)
       (mor_right_of_span C l₁)
       (mor_left_of_span C l₂)) =
PullbackArrow (comp_span_Pullback C PC k₁ k₂)
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁ h₂)
  (PullbackPr1 (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁ h₂)
   · span_sqr_ob_mor C s₁)
  (PullbackPr2 (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁ h₂)
   · span_sqr_ob_mor C s₂)
  (mor_of_comp_span_mor_subproof C PC s₁ s₂)
· (PullbackArrow (comp_span_Pullback C PC l₁ l₂)
     (comp_span_Pullback C PC k₁ k₂)
     (PullbackPr1 (comp_span_Pullback C PC k₁ k₂)
      · span_sqr_ob_mor C s₁')
     (PullbackPr2 (comp_span_Pullback C PC k₁ k₂)
      · span_sqr_ob_mor C s₂')
     (mor_of_comp_span_mor_subproof C PC s₁' s₂')
   · PullbackPr2
       (PC y₃ (ob_of_span C l₁) (ob_of_span C l₂)
          (mor_right_of_span C l₁)
          (mor_left_of_span C l₂)))

        
C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
x₁, x₂, x₃, y₁, y₂, y₃, z₁, z₂, z₃: C
v₁: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
v₁': C ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
v₂: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
v₂': C ⟦ y₂, y₃ ⟧
v₃: C ⟦ z₁, z₂ ⟧
v₃': C ⟦ z₂, z₃ ⟧
h₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₁ y₁
h₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y₁ z₁
k₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₂ y₂
k₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y₂ z₂
l₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₃ y₃
l₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y₃ z₃
s₁: h₁ -->[ v₁ ][ v₂] k₁
s₁': k₁ -->[ v₁' ][ v₂'] l₁
s₂: h₂ -->[ v₂ ][ v₃] k₂
s₂': k₂ -->[ v₂' ][ v₃'] l₂
PullbackPr2 (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁ h₂)
· (pr1 s₂ · pr1 s₂') =
PullbackArrow (comp_span_Pullback C PC k₁ k₂)
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁ h₂)
  (PullbackPr1 (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁ h₂)
   · span_sqr_ob_mor C s₁)
  (PullbackPr2 (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁ h₂)
   · span_sqr_ob_mor C s₂)
  (mor_of_comp_span_mor_subproof C PC s₁ s₂)
· (PullbackPr2 (comp_span_Pullback C PC k₁ k₂)
   · span_sqr_ob_mor C s₂')

        
C: category
PC: Pullbacks C

v₁: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
v₁': C ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
v₂: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
v₂': C ⟦ y₂, y₃ ⟧
v₃: C ⟦ z₁, z₂ ⟧
v₃': C ⟦ z₂, z₃ ⟧
h₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₁ y₁

s₂: h₂ -->[ v₂ ][ v₃] k₂

PullbackPr2 (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁ h₂) · pr1 s₂
· pr1 s₂' =

  (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁ h₂)
  (PullbackPr1 (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁ h₂)
   · span_sqr_ob_mor C s₁)

   · span_sqr_ob_mor C s₂)
  (mor_of_comp_span_mor_subproof C PC s₁ s₂)
· PullbackPr2 (comp_span_Pullback C PC k₁ k₂)
· span_sqr_ob_mor C s₂'

        apply idpath.
  Qed.

C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: C
h₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₁ y₁
h₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₂ y₂
v₁: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
v₂: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
sq: h₁ -->[ v₁ ][ v₂] h₂
trb₂ (spans_double_cat_lunitor_data x₁ y₁ h₁ ;;2 sq) =
double_hor_comp_mor spans_double_cat_hor_comp
  (double_id_mor spans_double_cat_hor_id v₁) sq ;;2 
spans_double_cat_lunitor_data x₂ y₂ h₂

    
C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: C

h₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₂ y₂
v₁: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
v₂: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
sq: h₁ -->[ v₁ ][ v₂] h₂
span_sqr_ob_mor C
  (trb₂ (spans_double_cat_lunitor_data x₁ y₁ h₁ ;;2 sq)) =
span_sqr_ob_mor C
  (double_hor_comp_mor spans_double_cat_hor_comp
     (double_id_mor spans_double_cat_hor_id v₁) sq ;;2 
   spans_double_cat_lunitor_data x₂ y₂ h₂)

    
C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: C
h₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₁ y₁
h₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₂ y₂

sq: h₁ -->[ v₁ ][ v₂] h₂
span_lunitor_mor C PC h₁ · pr1 sq =
mor_of_comp_span_mor C PC (id_span_mor C v₁) sq
· span_lunitor_mor C PC h₂

    
C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: C
h₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₁ y₁
h₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₂ y₂
v₁: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
v₂: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
sq: h₁ -->[ v₁ ][ v₂] h₂
PullbackPr2
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC (id_span C x₁) h₁) · pr1 sq =
PullbackArrow
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC (id_span C x₂) h₂)
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC (id_span C x₁) h₁)
  (PullbackPr1
     (comp_span_Pullback C PC (id_span C x₁) h₁)
   · span_sqr_ob_mor C (id_span_mor C v₁))
  (PullbackPr2
     (comp_span_Pullback C PC (id_span C x₁) h₁)
   · span_sqr_ob_mor C sq)
  (mor_of_comp_span_mor_subproof C PC
     (id_span_mor C v₁) sq)
· PullbackPr2
    (comp_span_Pullback C PC (id_span C x₂) h₂)

· span_sqr_ob_mor C sq

    apply idpath.
  Qed.

C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂: C

h₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₂ y₂
v₁: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
v₂: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
sq: h₁ -->[ v₁ ][ v₂] h₂
span_sqr_ob_mor C
  (trb₂ (spans_double_cat_runitor_data x₁ y₁ h₁ ;;2 sq)) =
span_sqr_ob_mor C
  (double_hor_comp_mor spans_double_cat_hor_comp sq
     (double_id_mor spans_double_cat_hor_id v₂) ;;2 
   spans_double_cat_runitor_data x₂ y₂ h₂)

v₁: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
v₂: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
sq: h₁ -->[ v₁ ][ v₂] h₂
span_runitor_mor C PC h₁ · pr1 sq =
mor_of_comp_span_mor C PC sq (id_span_mor C v₂)
· span_runitor_mor C PC h₂

v₁: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧

sq: h₁ -->[ v₁ ][ v₂] h₂
PullbackPr1
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁ (id_span C y₁)) · pr1 sq =
PullbackArrow
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂ (id_span C y₂))
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁ (id_span C y₁))
  (PullbackPr1
     (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁ (id_span C y₁))
   · span_sqr_ob_mor C sq)
  (PullbackPr2
     (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁ (id_span C y₁))
   · span_sqr_ob_mor C (id_span_mor C v₂))
  (mor_of_comp_span_mor_subproof C PC sq
     (id_span_mor C v₂))
· PullbackPr1
    (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂ (id_span C y₂))

    apply idpath.
  Qed.

C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
w₁, w₂, x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂, z₁, z₂: C
h₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C w₁ x₁
h₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C w₂ x₂
j₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₁ y₁
j₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₂ y₂
k₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y₁ z₁
k₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y₂ z₂
vw: C ⟦ w₁, w₂ ⟧
vx: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
vy: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
vz: C ⟦ z₁, z₂ ⟧
sq₁: h₁ -->[ vw ][ vx] h₂
sq₂: j₁ -->[ vx ][ vy] j₂
sq₃: k₁ -->[ vy ][ vz] k₂
PullbackArrow
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC (comp_span C PC h₁ j₁) k₁)
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁ (comp_span C PC j₁ k₁))
  (PullbackArrow (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁ j₁)
     (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁
        (comp_span C PC j₁ k₁))
     (PullbackPr1
        (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁
           (comp_span C PC j₁ k₁)))
     (PullbackPr2
        (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁
           (comp_span C PC j₁ k₁))
      · PullbackPr1 (comp_span_Pullback C PC j₁ k₁))
     (span_associator_mor_subproof C PC h₁ j₁ k₁))
  (PullbackPr2
     (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁
        (comp_span C PC j₁ k₁))
   · PullbackPr2 (comp_span_Pullback C PC j₁ k₁))
  (span_associator_mor_subproof0 C PC h₁ j₁ k₁)
· (PullbackArrow
     (comp_span_Pullback C PC (comp_span C PC h₂ j₂)
        k₂)
     (comp_span_Pullback C PC (comp_span C PC h₁ j₁)
        k₁)
     (PullbackPr1
        (comp_span_Pullback C PC
           (comp_span C PC h₁ j₁) k₁)
      · mor_of_comp_span_mor C PC sq₁ sq₂)
     (PullbackPr2
        (comp_span_Pullback C PC
           (comp_span C PC h₁ j₁) k₁)
      · span_sqr_ob_mor C sq₃)
     (mor_of_comp_span_mor_subproof C PC
        (comp_span_mor C PC sq₁ sq₂) sq₃)
   · PullbackPr1
       (PC y₂ (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂ j₂)
          (ob_of_span C k₂)
          (PullbackPr2 (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂ j₂)
           · mor_right_of_span C j₂)
          (mor_left_of_span C k₂))) =
PullbackArrow
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂ (comp_span C PC j₂ k₂))
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁ (comp_span C PC j₁ k₁))
  (PullbackPr1
     (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁
        (comp_span C PC j₁ k₁))
   · span_sqr_ob_mor C sq₁)
  (PullbackPr2
     (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁
        (comp_span C PC j₁ k₁))
   · mor_of_comp_span_mor C PC sq₂ sq₃)
  (mor_of_comp_span_mor_subproof C PC sq₁
     (comp_span_mor C PC sq₂ sq₃))
· (PullbackArrow
     (comp_span_Pullback C PC (comp_span C PC h₂ j₂)
        k₂)
     (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂
        (comp_span C PC j₂ k₂))
     (PullbackArrow (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂ j₂)
        (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂

h₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C w₁ x₁
h₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C w₂ x₂
j₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₁ y₁
j₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₂ y₂
k₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y₁ z₁
k₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y₂ z₂
vw: C ⟦ w₁, w₂ ⟧
vx: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
vy: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
vz: C ⟦ z₁, z₂ ⟧
sq₁: h₁ -->[ vw ][ vx] h₂
sq₂: j₁ -->[ vx ][ vy] j₂
sq₃: k₁ -->[ vy ][ vz] k₂
PullbackPr2
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁ (comp_span C PC j₁ k₁))
· PullbackPr1 (comp_span_Pullback C PC j₁ k₁)
· span_sqr_ob_mor C sq₂ =
PullbackPr2
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁ (comp_span C PC j₁ k₁))
· PullbackArrow (comp_span_Pullback C PC j₂ k₂)
    (comp_span_Pullback C PC j₁ k₁)
    (PullbackPr1 (comp_span_Pullback C PC j₁ k₁)
     · span_sqr_ob_mor C sq₂)
    (PullbackPr2 (comp_span_Pullback C PC j₁ k₁)
     · span_sqr_ob_mor C sq₃)
    (mor_of_comp_span_mor_subproof C PC sq₂ sq₃)
· PullbackPr1 (comp_span_Pullback C PC j₂ k₂)

· mor_of_comp_span_mor C PC
    (comp_span_mor C PC sq₁ sq₂) sq₃
· PullbackPr2
    (PC y₂ (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂ j₂)
       (ob_of_span C k₂)
       (PullbackPr2 (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂ j₂)
        · mor_right_of_span C j₂)
       (mor_left_of_span C k₂)) =

· span_associator_mor C PC h₂ j₂ k₂

       (ob_of_span C k₂)
       (PullbackPr2 (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂ j₂)
        · mor_right_of_span C j₂)

     (comp_span_mor C PC sq₁ sq₂) sq₃

PC: Pullbacks C
w₁, w₂, x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂, z₁, z₂: C
h₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C w₁ x₁
h₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C w₂ x₂
j₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₁ y₁
j₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₂ y₂
k₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y₁ z₁
k₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y₂ z₂
vw: C ⟦ w₁, w₂ ⟧
vx: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
vy: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
vz: C ⟦ z₁, z₂ ⟧
sq₁: h₁ -->[ vw ][ vx] h₂
sq₂: j₁ -->[ vx ][ vy] j₂
sq₃: k₁ -->[ vy ][ vz] k₂
PullbackArrow
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC (comp_span C PC h₁ j₁) k₁)
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁ (comp_span C PC j₁ k₁))
  (PullbackArrow (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁ j₁)
     (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁
        (comp_span C PC j₁ k₁))
     (PullbackPr1
        (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁
           (comp_span C PC j₁ k₁)))
     (PullbackPr2
        (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁
           (comp_span C PC j₁ k₁))
      · PullbackPr1 (comp_span_Pullback C PC j₁ k₁))
     (span_associator_mor_subproof C PC h₁ j₁ k₁))
  (PullbackPr2
     (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁
        (comp_span C PC j₁ k₁))
   · PullbackPr2 (comp_span_Pullback C PC j₁ k₁))
  (span_associator_mor_subproof0 C PC h₁ j₁ k₁)
· (PullbackArrow
     (comp_span_Pullback C PC (comp_span C PC h₂ j₂)
        k₂)
     (comp_span_Pullback C PC (comp_span C PC h₁ j₁)
        k₁)
     (PullbackPr1
        (comp_span_Pullback C PC
           (comp_span C PC h₁ j₁) k₁)
      · mor_of_comp_span_mor C PC sq₁ sq₂)
     (PullbackPr2
        (comp_span_Pullback C PC
           (comp_span C PC h₁ j₁) k₁)
      · span_sqr_ob_mor C sq₃)
     (mor_of_comp_span_mor_subproof C PC
        (comp_span_mor C PC sq₁ sq₂) sq₃)
   · PullbackPr2
       (PC y₂ (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂ j₂)
          (ob_of_span C k₂)
          (PullbackPr2 (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂ j₂)
           · mor_right_of_span C j₂)
          (mor_left_of_span C k₂))) =
PullbackArrow
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂ (comp_span C PC j₂ k₂))
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁ (comp_span C PC j₁ k₁))
  (PullbackPr1
     (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁
        (comp_span C PC j₁ k₁))
   · span_sqr_ob_mor C sq₁)
  (PullbackPr2
     (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁
        (comp_span C PC j₁ k₁))
   · mor_of_comp_span_mor C PC sq₂ sq₃)
  (mor_of_comp_span_mor_subproof C PC sq₁
     (comp_span_mor C PC sq₂ sq₃))
· (PullbackArrow
     (comp_span_Pullback C PC (comp_span C PC h₂ j₂)
        k₂)
     (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂
        (comp_span C PC j₂ k₂))
     (PullbackArrow (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂ j₂)
        (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂
           (comp_span C PC j₂ k₂))
        (PullbackPr1
           (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂
              (comp_span C PC j₂ k₂)))
        (PullbackPr2
           (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂
              (comp_span C PC j₂ k₂))
         · PullbackPr1 (comp_span_Pullback C PC j₂ k₂))
        (span_associator_mor_subproof C PC h₂ j₂ k₂))
     (PullbackPr2
        (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂
           (comp_span C PC j₂ k₂))
      · PullbackPr2 (comp_span_Pullback C PC j₂ k₂))
     (span_associator_mor_subproof0 C PC h₂ j₂ k₂)
   · PullbackPr2
       (PC y₂ (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂ j₂)
          (ob_of_span C k₂)
          (PullbackPr2 (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂ j₂)
           · mor_right_of_span C j₂)
          (mor_left_of_span C k₂)))

     (comp_span_mor C PC sq₂ sq₃))

     (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂
        (comp_span C PC j₂ k₂))
   · PullbackPr2 (comp_span_Pullback C PC j₂ k₂))

h₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C w₂ x₂
j₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₁ y₁
j₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₂ y₂
k₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y₁ z₁
k₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y₂ z₂
vw: C ⟦ w₁, w₂ ⟧
vx: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
vy: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
vz: C ⟦ z₁, z₂ ⟧
sq₁: h₁ -->[ vw ][ vx] h₂
sq₂: j₁ -->[ vx ][ vy] j₂
sq₃: k₁ -->[ vy ][ vz] k₂
PullbackPr2 (comp_span_Pullback C PC j₁ k₁)
· span_sqr_ob_mor C sq₃ =
PullbackArrow (comp_span_Pullback C PC j₂ k₂)
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC j₁ k₁)
  (PullbackPr1 (comp_span_Pullback C PC j₁ k₁)
   · span_sqr_ob_mor C sq₂)
  (PullbackPr2 (comp_span_Pullback C PC j₁ k₁)
   · span_sqr_ob_mor C sq₃)
  (mor_of_comp_span_mor_subproof C PC sq₂ sq₃)
· PullbackPr2 (comp_span_Pullback C PC j₂ k₂)

      
C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
w₁, w₂, x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂, z₁, z₂: C
h₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C w₁ x₁
h₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C w₂ x₂
j₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₁ y₁
j₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x₂ y₂
k₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y₁ z₁
k₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y₂ z₂
vw: C ⟦ w₁, w₂ ⟧
vx: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
vy: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
vz: C ⟦ z₁, z₂ ⟧
sq₁: h₁ -->[ vw ][ vx] h₂
sq₂: j₁ -->[ vx ][ vy] j₂
sq₃: k₁ -->[ vy ][ vz] k₂
PullbackPr2 (comp_span_Pullback C PC j₁ k₁)
· span_sqr_ob_mor C sq₃ =
PullbackPr2 (comp_span_Pullback C PC j₁ k₁)
· span_sqr_ob_mor C sq₃

      apply idpath.
  Qed.

double_associator spans_double_cat_associator h
  (double_id spans_double_cat_hor_id y) k ;;2 double_hor_comp_mor
                                                spans_double_cat_hor_comp
                                                (double_runitor
                                                 spans_double_cat_runitor
                                                 h)
                                                (id_two_disp
                                                 k) =

       (id_two_disp h)
       (double_lunitor spans_double_cat_lunitor k)

  (double_associator spans_double_cat_associator h
     (double_id spans_double_cat_hor_id y) k ;;2 double_hor_comp_mor
                                                 spans_double_cat_hor_comp

      Core.id_disp (pr12 h₁),, Core.id_disp (pr22 h₁))
     (span_associator C PC h₂ h₃ h₄))
· PullbackPr2
    (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁
       (comp_span C PC (comp_span C PC h₂ h₃) h₄))
· PullbackPr2
    (comp_span_Pullback C PC (comp_span C PC h₂ h₃) h₄)
· id₁ (pr1 h₄) =
PullbackPr2
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁
     (comp_span C PC h₂ (comp_span C PC h₃ h₄)))
· PullbackPr2
    (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂ (comp_span C PC h₃ h₄))
· PullbackPr2 (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₃ h₄)

      
C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
v, w, x, y, z: C
h₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C v w
h₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C w x
h₃: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x y
h₄: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y z
PullbackArrow
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁
     (comp_span C PC (comp_span C PC h₂ h₃) h₄))
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁
     (comp_span C PC h₂ (comp_span C PC h₃ h₄)))
  (PullbackPr1
     (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁
        (comp_span C PC h₂ (comp_span C PC h₃ h₄)))
   · id₁ (pr1 h₁))
  (PullbackPr2
     (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁
        (comp_span C PC h₂ (comp_span C PC h₃ h₄)))
   · span_associator_mor C PC h₂ h₃ h₄)
  (mor_of_comp_span_mor_subproof C PC
     (id₁ (pr1 h₁),,
      Core.id_disp (pr12 h₁),, Core.id_disp (pr22 h₁))
     (span_associator C PC h₂ h₃ h₄))
· PullbackPr2
    (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁
       (comp_span C PC (comp_span C PC h₂ h₃) h₄))
· PullbackPr2
    (comp_span_Pullback C PC (comp_span C PC h₂ h₃) h₄) =
PullbackPr2
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁
     (comp_span C PC h₂ (comp_span C PC h₃ h₄)))
· PullbackPr2
    (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂ (comp_span C PC h₃ h₄))
· PullbackPr2 (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₃ h₄)

      
C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
v, w, x, y, z: C
h₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C v w
h₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C w x
h₃: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x y
h₄: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y z
PullbackPr2
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁
     (comp_span C PC h₂ (comp_span C PC h₃ h₄)))
· span_associator_mor C PC h₂ h₃ h₄
· PullbackPr2
    (comp_span_Pullback C PC (comp_span C PC h₂ h₃) h₄) =
PullbackPr2
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁
     (comp_span C PC h₂ (comp_span C PC h₃ h₄)))
· PullbackPr2
    (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂ (comp_span C PC h₃ h₄))

C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
v, w, x, y, z: C
h₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C v w
h₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C w x
h₃: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x y
h₄: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y z
PullbackPr2
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁
     (comp_span C PC h₂ (comp_span C PC h₃ h₄)))
· PullbackArrow
    (comp_span_Pullback C PC (comp_span C PC h₂ h₃) h₄)
    (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂ (comp_span C PC h₃ h₄))
    (PullbackArrow (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂ h₃)
       (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂
          (comp_span C PC h₃ h₄))
       (PullbackPr1
          (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂
             (comp_span C PC h₃ h₄)))
       (PullbackPr2
          (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂
             (comp_span C PC h₃ h₄))
        · PullbackPr1 (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₃ h₄))
       (span_associator_mor_subproof C PC h₂ h₃ h₄))
    (PullbackPr2
       (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂
          (comp_span C PC h₃ h₄))
     · PullbackPr2 (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₃ h₄))
    (span_associator_mor_subproof0 C PC h₂ h₃ h₄)
· PullbackPr2
    (comp_span_Pullback C PC (comp_span C PC h₂ h₃) h₄) =
PullbackPr2
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁
     (comp_span C PC h₂ (comp_span C PC h₃ h₄)))
· PullbackPr2
    (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂ (comp_span C PC h₃ h₄))
· PullbackPr2 (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₃ h₄)

      
C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
v, w, x, y, z: C
h₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C v w
h₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C w x
h₃: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x y
h₄: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y z
PullbackPr2
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁
     (comp_span C PC h₂ (comp_span C PC h₃ h₄)))
· (PullbackArrow
     (comp_span_Pullback C PC (comp_span C PC h₂ h₃)
        h₄)
     (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂
        (comp_span C PC h₃ h₄))
     (PullbackArrow (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂ h₃)
        (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂
           (comp_span C PC h₃ h₄))
        (PullbackPr1
           (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂
              (comp_span C PC h₃ h₄)))
        (PullbackPr2
           (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂
              (comp_span C PC h₃ h₄))
         · PullbackPr1 (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₃ h₄))
        (span_associator_mor_subproof C PC h₂ h₃ h₄))
     (PullbackPr2
        (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂
           (comp_span C PC h₃ h₄))
      · PullbackPr2 (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₃ h₄))
     (span_associator_mor_subproof0 C PC h₂ h₃ h₄)
   · PullbackPr2
       (comp_span_Pullback C PC (comp_span C PC h₂ h₃)
          h₄)) =
PullbackPr2
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁
     (comp_span C PC h₂ (comp_span C PC h₃ h₄)))
· (PullbackPr2
     (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂
        (comp_span C PC h₃ h₄))
   · PullbackPr2 (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₃ h₄))

      
C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
v, w, x, y, z: C
h₁: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C v w
h₂: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C w x
h₃: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C x y
h₄: twosided_disp_cat_of_spans C y z
PullbackPr2
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁
     (comp_span C PC h₂ (comp_span C PC h₃ h₄)))
· (PullbackPr2
     (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂
        (comp_span C PC h₃ h₄))
   · PullbackPr2 (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₃ h₄)) =
PullbackPr2
  (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₁
     (comp_span C PC h₂ (comp_span C PC h₃ h₄)))
· (PullbackPr2
     (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₂
        (comp_span C PC h₃ h₄))
   · PullbackPr2 (comp_span_Pullback C PC h₃ h₄))

      apply idpath.
  Qed.

  (id_v_right (identity_v x ·v identity_v x) @
   id_v_right (identity_v x))
  (id_v_right (identity_v y ·v identity_v y) @
   id_v_right (identity_v y))
  (linvunitor_h (span_companion C f)
   ⋆v span_companion_counit C f
      ⋆h span_companion_unit C f
   ⋆v runitor_h (span_companion C f)) =
id_v_square (span_companion C f)
 abstract
          (use span_sqr_eq ;
           refine (transportf_disp_mor2_span _ _ _ _ @ _) ;
           cbn ;
           unfold mor_of_comp_span_mor, span_runitor_mor, span_linvunitor ;
           rewrite !assoc' ;
           rewrite PullbackArrow_PullbackPr1 ;
           rewrite !assoc ;
           rewrite PullbackArrow_PullbackPr1 ;
           cbn ;
           apply id_left).

  Defined.

  (id_v_left (identity_v x · identity_v x) @
   id_v_left (identity_v x))
  (rinvunitor_h (span_conjoint C f)
   ⋆v (span_conjoint_counit C f
       ⋆h span_conjoint_unit C f
       ⋆v lunitor_h (span_conjoint C f))) =
id_v_square (span_conjoint C f)
 abstract
          (use span_sqr_eq ;
           refine (transportf_disp_mor2_span _ _ _ _ @ _) ;
           cbn ;
           unfold mor_of_comp_span_mor, span_lunitor_mor, span_rinvunitor ;
           rewrite PullbackArrow_PullbackPr2 ;
           rewrite !assoc ;
           rewrite PullbackArrow_PullbackPr2 ;
           cbn ;
           apply id_left).
      
C: category
PC: Pullbacks C
x, y: spans_double_cat
f: x -->v y
transportf_square (id_v_right f) (id_v_left f)
  (span_conjoint_unit C f ⋆v span_conjoint_counit C f) =
id_h_square f
 abstract
          (use span_sqr_eq ;
           refine (transportf_disp_mor2_span _ _ _ _ @ _) ;
           cbn ;
           apply id_left).
  Defined.
End SpansDoubleCat.
